name

Mac NID 8/13

License text.

There is a license text but no manufactur. Please verify agains spec.
The license text is:
Microsoft supplied font. You may use this font to create, display, and print content as permitted by the license terms or terms of use, of the Microsoft product, service, or content in which this font was included. You may only (i) embed this font in content as permitted by the embedding restrictions included in this font; and (ii) temporarily download this font to a printer or other output device to help print content. Any other use is prohibited.

Pass

TH SarabunPSK Regular (thsarabun.ttf)

name

Mac NID 16/17

If NID 2 and 17 = 'Regular': Mac NID 16 should match NID 1.
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). This is true for MS Office Version 1639 and lower. Even though Microsoft has changed it with version 1640 (fast insider, June 2020) we keep this as an error, because most of the current MS Office users won't update in the near future. More infos here:
Cross Platform Issues

NID 16 'TH SarabunPSK' = NID 1 'TH SarabunPSK'.

Pass

MS NID 0 (3, 1, 1033, 0)

MS NID 0, Copyright.

Please verify agains spec.
MS NID 0 is 'Copyright (c) 2006 by Department of Intellectual Property (DIP), Ministry of Commerce and Software Industry Promotion Agency (Public Organization) (SIPA), with Reserved Font Name “TH SarabunPSK”.'
It should follow this structure: 'Copyright (c) XXXX - XXXX /entity/. All rights reserved.'

License text.

Microsoft supplied font. You may use this font to create, display, and print content as permitted by the license terms or terms of use, of the Microsoft product, service, or content in which this font was included. You may only (i) embed this font in content as permitted by the embedding restrictions included in this font; and (ii) temporarily download this font to a printer or other output device to help print content. Any other use is prohibited.

TH SarabunPSK Italic (thsarabun-italic.ttf)

name

Mac NID 16/17

Mac NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'TH SarabunPSK' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Italic' = NID 1 'TH SarabunPSK' + 'Space' + NID 2 'Italic'.

Pass

TH SarabunPSK Bold (thsarabun-bold.ttf)

name

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'THSarabunPSK-Bold', Everything looks good.

Pass

TH SarabunPSK Bold (thsarabun-bold.ttf)

name

Mac NID 16/17

Mac NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'TH SarabunPSK' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Bold' = NID 1 'TH SarabunPSK' + 'Space' + NID 2 'Bold'.

Pass

TH SarabunPSK Bold (thsarabun-bold.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'THSarabunPSK-Bold', Everything looks good.

Pass

TH SarabunPSK Bold (thsarabun-bold.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'TH SarabunPSK' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Bold' = NID 1 'TH SarabunPSK' + 'Space' + NID 2 'Bold'.

Pass

Kerning (kern Table and GPOS Kerning)

Kerning (kern Table and GPOS Kerning)

Pass

TH SarabunPSK Regular (thsarabun.ttf)

GPOS

kern

Simple check if kern feature in GPOS table.

The font has GPOS kerning.

Warning

TH SarabunPSK Regular (thsarabun.ttf)

kern

-/-

Check if 'kern' table in TTF font.

Font has 'kern' table. Please verify if font requires kern table or if only GPOS kerning should be in font.
For example: PowerPoint only supports a flat GPOS kerning or a kern table. So, if the customer requires PowerPoint support, a kern table is necessary.

Default

Grid-fit = True, Do gray = True
and should be:
Grid-fit = True, Do gray = True, Symmetric grid-fit = True, Symmetric smoothing = True

TH SarabunPSK Regular (thsarabun.ttf)

gasp
